# Mining Speed and Block Breaking Mechanics

## Breaking Speed Formula
- Ticks = round( (Block_Strength * 30) / Mining_Speed )
- 1 tick = 0.05 seconds (20 ticks per second)
- Softcap (minimum without instant-mine) is always 4 ticks (0.2s)
- Between softcap (4-tick) and instant mine (1-tick), there is NOTHING — no 3-tick or 2-tick. It jumps from 4 directly to 1.
- Instant mine for ores: Mining_Speed >= 60 * Block_Strength + 1
- Instant mine for non-ores (hard stone, cobble): Mining_Speed >= 30 * Block_Strength + 1

## Mithril Mining Speed Thresholds

### Gray Mithril (Block Strength ~500)
- 5 ticks: > 2,728 Mining Speed
- 4 ticks (softcap): > 3,334 Mining Speed
- Instant mine (1 tick): > 30,000 Mining Speed

### Green/Prismarine Mithril (Block Strength ~800)
- 8 ticks: > 2,824 Mining Speed
- 7 ticks: > 3,201 Mining Speed
- 6 ticks: > 3,693 Mining Speed
- 5 ticks: > 4,364 Mining Speed
- 4 ticks (softcap): > 5,334 Mining Speed
- Instant mine (1 tick): > 48,000 Mining Speed

### Blue Mithril (Block Strength ~1,500)
- 12 ticks: > 3,600 Mining Speed
- 10 ticks: > 4,286 Mining Speed
- 8 ticks: > 5,295 Mining Speed
- 6 ticks: > 6,924 Mining Speed
- 5 ticks: > 8,182 Mining Speed
- 4 ticks (softcap): > 10,000 Mining Speed
- Instant mine (1 tick): > 90,000 Mining Speed

### Titanium (spawns from mithril)
- 8 ticks: > 7,059 Mining Speed

### Gemstones (Block Strength ~3,000-5,000)
- Softcap (4 ticks) for Gemstones: ~20,000-33,334 Mining Speed depending on type

## Key Notes
- "4-tick mithril" means reaching the softcap — the fastest possible mining speed before instant mine.
- For gray mithril, you need > 3,334 Mining Speed to 4-tick it.
- For blue mithril (hardest), you need > 10,000 Mining Speed to 4-tick it.
- Most players asking about "4-tick mithril" mean gray mithril (> 3,334 Mining Speed).

# Divan's Armor

Redirect to:
- Armor of Divan

# Mineral Armor

Mineral Armor is an EPIC Armor set that increases the amount of blocks with Ⓟ Breaking Power of 3 or less that the player can mine with a Pickaxe . This armor is crafted with Refined Minerals , which drop from Ores during the Mining Fiesta event when Cole 's Mining Fiesta perk is active.

### Tiered Bonus
Similar to the Efficient Miner perk in the Heart of the Mountain that grants ▚ Mining Spread , Mineral Armor grants extra ▚ Mining Spread on Ores and Blocks .

## Trivia
- It was once possible to obtain a Dungeon Armor version of this set by turning the base Hardened Diamond Armor into a dungeon item via Essence Crafting.
- This set was best used for leveling up Mining by mining End Stone in the End . When using this method, it was best to use a Stonk so that Endermites didn't spawn. This method could result in up to +600,000 Mining XP per hour. However, since the introduction of the ⏣ Dwarven Mines and ⏣ Crystal Hollows , mining Mithril or completing commissions is much more efficient.
- Although it isn't stated in the armor itself, the Mineral Armor special effect does not work on private islands.

# Divan's Drill

The Divan's Drill is a MYTHIC Drill .

## Stats
  Drill V E D
  Divan's Drill ❁ Damage : +75 ☘ Mining Fortune : +150 Ⓟ Breaking Power : +10 ⸕ Mining Speed : +1,800
- ❁ Damage : +75
- ☘ Mining Fortune : +150
- Ⓟ Breaking Power : +10
- ⸕ Mining Speed : +1,800

## Obtaining
The Divan's Drill can be forged once the player has reached Heart of the Mountain VII . It takes 30 seconds to forge.

## Usage
The Divan's Drill has a base ♢ Fuel of 3,000 , which can be increased through a Fuel Tank . Additionally, a Drill Engine and Upgrade Module can be added to the drill through a Drill Anvil to grant further bonuses.
When breaking blocks, the Divan's Drill 's ♢ Fuel will deplete. Most resources will remove 1 ♢ Fuel when mined; Aquamarine , Citrine , Onyx and Peridot remove 2 ♢ Fuel instead; Glacite , Umber and Tungsten remove 3 ♢ Fuel instead. ♢ Fuel can be regained by adding Fuel to the Drill through a Drill Anvil .

## Tips
- The 5th slot of the drill is Mining, and can have Topaz as well as Jade or Amber applied to it.

## Trivia
- It is the third item that has a base MYTHIC rarity, after the Plasma Bucket and Cake Souls
- This item requires the fourth highest amount of raw materials at 12,027,076.
- The total time it takes to forge the drill and all of its components is 3438 hours (143 days 6 hours), or 2406.6 hours (100 days 6.6 hours) with Quick Forge 20.
- Prior 0.17.2, Divan's Drill was needed to obtain the Kuudra Relic . The requirement has been changed to any Drill .
- Divan's Drill is tied in fourth for having the most gemstone slots with Mastiff Armor , Armor of Divan and Gemstone Gauntlet , with all of the aforementioned falling behind the Artifact of Power , Relic of Power , and Shimmersparkle Chestplate .

# Pickonimbus 2000

The Pickonimbus 2000 is an EPIC Pickaxe .

## Stats
  Pickaxe V E D
  Pickonimbus 2000 Ⓟ Breaking Power : +8 ⸕ Mining Speed : +750 ❁ Damage : +30
- Ⓟ Breaking Power : +8
- ⸕ Mining Speed : +750
- ❁ Damage : +30
  Effects
  A powerful tool that breaks after 2000 uses.

## Obtaining
A Pickonimbus 2000 has a 37.48% to 48.89% chance to appear in a ⏣ Crystal Nucleus loot bundle. It also has a 0.14% chance to appear in a Treasure Chest . There is a 0.07% chance for it to be found when using a Metal Detector in the ⏣ Mines of Divan when having found all Scavenged Items and a 0.06% chance when not having found all Scavenged Items .

## Usage
The Pickonimbus 2000 requires Heart of the Mountain IV to use.

### Salvaging
Pickonimbus 2000 can be salvaged for 5x Diamond Essence .

## Trivia
- The Pickonimbus 2000 is a reference to the Nimbus 2000 broomstick from the Harry Potter franchise.
- This is the only pickaxe to have durability.
- The pickaxe does not have a durability bar even though it breaks after 2,000 uses. Instead, the number of uses left is displayed in the lore.
- A Pickonimbus 2000 can be repaired to full durability in an Anvil by placing a brand new unenchanted Pickonimbus in the first slot and the damaged one in the second slot. It will transfer over enchantments, but not reforges. However, it resets the Compact counter (but not the enchantment's level), making 4 the highest level attainable on a Pickonimbus 2000 that didn't already have a higher level before SkyBlock 0.19.1.
- Unlike Drill Fuel, blocks mined by ▚ Mining Spread and abilities that break multiple blocks at once (such as Pickobulus) also remove durability from the Pickonimbus 2000 .
- It is not possible to auction a Pickonimbus 2000 below 2,000 durability, but they can still be traded.
- In the SkyBlock 0.20.6 update, existing Pickonimbus 2000 s that were at full durability were reduced to 2,000 durability, but ones that were between 2,001 and 4,999 durability kept their extra durability. This is because Pickonimbuses at full durability do not have a pickonimbus_durability tag in their NBT data, and damaged ones were not modified. This update also resulted in Pickonimbuses with more than 2,000 but less than 5,000 durability becoming auctionable.
- This is because Pickonimbuses at full durability do not have a pickonimbus_durability tag in their NBT data, and damaged ones were not modified.
- This update also resulted in Pickonimbuses with more than 2,000 but less than 5,000 durability becoming auctionable.

  Increased Ⓟ Breaking Power from 7 Ⓟ to 8 Ⓟ .

  Damaged Pickonimbus 2000 s can no longer be auctioned.

## Kat Caretaking Costs
Kat can upgrade all rarities of this pet .
- For each level the pet has, there is a 0.3% discount.
- The time listed is in real life days, not in-game time. ## Trivia
- On islands with custom mining mechanics, such as the Dwarven Mines , the Haste effect does not apply, and is converted into extra ⸕ Mining Speed instead.

# Mithril Golem Pet

The Mithril Golem Pet is a Mining Pet unlocked at Mithril III . The crafting recipe requires 256x Mithril and an Enchanted Egg . The LEGENDARY variant can be upgraded to MYTHIC by Kat in exchange for 100,000 coins and a Pure Mithril Gem .
The Mithril Golem Pet is good for those looking to spend a lot of time in the ⏣ Dwarven Mines . Its abilities provide a boost to ⸕ Mining Speed while mining Mithril , increases ᠅ Mithril Powder gained from all sources, and gives increased Combat stats and ✯ Magic Find to players on Mining Islands for those looking to fight the monsters.

## Crafting
  Requirements
  Ingredients
  Crafting Recipe
  Mithril III
  256x Mithril 1x Enchanted Egg
- 256x Mithril
- 1x Enchanted Egg
  32 32 32 32 32 32 32 32

## Kat Caretaking Costs
Kat can upgrade all rarities of this pet .
- For each level the pet has, there is a 0.3% discount.
- The time listed is in real life days, not in-game time. ## Trivia
- The LEGENDARY variant's 2nd perk boosts Combat stats on Mining Islands. Affected Combat stats include: ❤ Health ❈ Defense ❁ Strength ☣ Crit Chance ☠ Crit Damage Mining Islands include: Gold Mine Deep Caverns , with the sub-locations: Gunpowder Mines Lapis Quarry Pigmen's Den Slimehill Diamond Reserve Obsidian Sanctuary Dwarven Mines Crystal Hollows Glacite Tunnels Glacite Mineshafts
- Affected Combat stats include: ❤ Health ❈ Defense ❁ Strength ☣ Crit Chance ☠ Crit Damage
- ❤ Health
- ❈ Defense
- ❁ Strength
- ☣ Crit Chance
- ☠ Crit Damage
- Mining Islands include: Gold Mine Deep Caverns , with the sub-locations: Gunpowder Mines Lapis Quarry Pigmen's Den Slimehill Diamond Reserve Obsidian Sanctuary Dwarven Mines Crystal Hollows Glacite Tunnels Glacite Mineshafts
- Gold Mine
- Deep Caverns , with the sub-locations: Gunpowder Mines Lapis Quarry Pigmen's Den Slimehill Diamond Reserve Obsidian Sanctuary
- Gunpowder Mines
- Lapis Quarry
- Pigmen's Den
- Slimehill
- Diamond Reserve
- Obsidian Sanctuary
- Dwarven Mines
- Crystal Hollows
- Glacite Tunnels
- Glacite Mineshafts
- Though this pet has the cheapest cost of upgrading from EPIC to LEGENDARY at Kat ( 200,000 coins , or 140,000 coins if Level 100), it has the longest wait times of any pet upgrade, at 20 days.
- This pet is one of the only pets which increases multiple stats by a percentage. The pet displays an increase of + 20% for all Combat stats, however the actual damage increase is much higher, due to it boosting both ❁ Strength and ☠ Crit Damage .
- The pet displays an increase of + 20% for all Combat stats, however the actual damage increase is much higher, due to it boosting both ❁ Strength and ☠ Crit Damage .
- The Mithril Golem Pet gives the most ❂ True Defense out of any pet in the game.

# Bal Pet

The Bal Pet is a Mining Pet obtained as a rare drop from Bal .

## Obtaining
There is a 0.0126% ( 1 in 7,937 hits) chance to obtain a EPIC Bal Pet , and a 0.0054% ( 1 in 18,519 hits) chance for a LEGENDARY Bal Pet . The overall chance to obtain any rarity is 0.018% ( 1 in 5,556 hits). These chances are not affected by ✯ Magic Find or ♣ Pet Luck .
Assuming Bal is fully killed and all 200 hits are from the same player, the chance for an EPIC Bal Pet is 2.52% ( 1 in 39.68 kills), the chance for a LEGENDARY Bal Pet is 1.08% ( 1 in 92.59 kills), and the chance for any rarity is 3.6% ( 1 in 27.78 kills).

## Stats
- Epic
- Legendary
  Starting Stats (Level 1) ⓘ
  Max Stats (Level 100) ⓘ V E D
  Stats: ♨ Heat Resistance : +1.5 ☘ Mining Fortune : +1 Abilities: Furnace - Grants 0.02 ✧ Pristine while in the Magma Fields . Dispersion - While in the Crystal Hollows , killing mobs reduces your ♨ Heat by 0.04 .
- ♨ Heat Resistance : +1.5
- ☘ Mining Fortune : +1
- Furnace - Grants 0.02 ✧ Pristine while in the Magma Fields .
- Dispersion - While in the Crystal Hollows , killing mobs reduces your ♨ Heat by 0.04 .

Kat can upgrade all rarities of this pet .

- The time listed is in real life days, not in-game time. Rarity Upgrade Cost Time Coins Materials EPIC → LEGENDARY 2M coins 100x Yoggie 10 Days

## Trivia
- The Bal Pet is inspired by the Balrog, a creature from Lord of the Rings .
- The Bal Pet can be given to George after reaching Taming 50 to increase the Taming level cap by 1.
- Multiple Bal Pets can be dropped by the same player from the same boss.
- The name Bal or Baal originates from proto-Semitic word for "owner" or "master". It got into English through Phoenician, Hebrew, Greek and Latin, where on top of the previously mentioned it gained the meaning "Lord". It is cognate with Beelzebub and Belphegor, two names for the Devil.

## References
- ↑ https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Baal#English

# Scatha Pet

The Scatha Pet is a Mining Pet that grants ☘ Mining Fortune and ⸕ Mining Speed to the player.

## Obtaining
It is rarely dropped from Scathas in the Crystal Hollows , found when mining Hard Stone .
- RARE Pet: 0.24%
- EPIC Pet: 0.12%
- LEGENDARY Pet: 0.04%

## Kat Caretaking Costs
Kat can upgrade all rarities of this pet .
- For each level the pet has, there is a 0.3% discount.
- The time listed is in real life days, not in-game time. Rarity Upgrade Cost Time Coins Materials RARE → EPIC 125M coins 64x Enchanted Hard Stone 7 days EPIC → LEGENDARY 250M coins 256x Enchanted Hard Stone 14 days

## Trivia
- The name "Scatha" is a reference to the wingless dragon Scatha in The Lord of the Rings .
- The Bejeweled Eyes ability is additive with the Powder Buff perk from the Heart of the Mountain .

# Mining

Mining is one of the ten non-cosmetic Skills available for players to level up as they perform certain actions that grant Mining experience.

## Ways to boost XP gain
The amount of Mining XP the player receives can be increased through the ☯ Mining Wisdom stat. The maximum possible Mining Wisdom that can be achieved is displayed below.
- Mayor Jerry [ Cole ]
- Mining Fiesta
- LEGENDARY Silverfish Pet [ [ Lv100 ] ]
- Divan's Drill [ Refined + Recombobulator 3000 + Compact X ]
- Booster Cookie
- Mining XP Boost III
- Seasoned Mineman 101
- Actually Blue™ Abicase

## Spelunker
Spelunker is an ability unlocked exclusively by leveling up the Mining Skill. Each level of Spelunker grants +4 ☘ Mining Fortune for almost any Mining XP-yielding block to drop 2-4x its original amount (2x Ore Drop at levels 1-25, 3x at levels 26–50, 4x at levels 51–60).
Each level of Mining grants one level of Spelunker. For example, if the player is on Mining level 15, they would be on Spelunker level 15, and the chance for x2 Ore Drop would be 60%.
The Spelunker perk does not apply to Redstone or Lapis Lazuli and does not influence how much ore is gained from mining it. This is believed to be a bug as much more Redstone and Lapis Lazuli is gained per ore than the others.

## Leveling Rewards
The cumulative rewards at Combat level 25 are:
- +100% additional Mob Damage
- +12.5% ☣ Crit Chance
- 1,334,100 coins
- 200 SkyBlock XP
The cumulative rewards at Combat level 50 are:
- +200% additional Mob Damage
- +25% ☣ Crit Chance

# Heart of the Mountain

This page is undergoing a review and will be updated frequently. Content on this page might change drastically during this review. To avoid edit conflicts, please avoid editing whilst this notice is present.
The Heart of the Mountain , commonly abbreviated as HotM , is a skill tree related to Mining .

## Unlocking
Heart of the Mountain is unlocked by completing Rhys quest in the ⏣ Obsidian Sanctuary , which requires 15 of any enchanted ore.
As players level up their Heart of the Mountain, they will gain Tokens of the Mountain , which can be used to unlock various perks. Some of these perks will take effect only on public islands with new mining mechanism (alongside with infinite Mining Fatigue).

## Mechanics
The menu can be accessed via the SkyBlock Menu , while inside the ⏣ Dwarven Mines and ⏣ Crystal Hollows , via the Mining menu, or anywhere via the /hotm command.
Players can level up their Heart of the Mountain tiers by gaining HotM experience, which can be accumulated by completing Commissions , participating in various active mining events and completing Crystal Nucleus runs.
Each Commission completed in the ⏣ Dwarven Mines or ⏣ Crystal Hollows gives up to 400 Heart of the Mountain experience, while Commissions completed in the ⏣ Glacite Tunnels give 750 Heart of the Mountain experience.
At Heart of the Mountain Tiers 1 and 2, experience from ⏣ Dwarven Mines commissions is 100 and 200 each, respectively, while at Tier 3 it becomes 400 , matching ⏣ Crystal Hollows .
Players receive additional 900 Heart of the Mountain experience for the first four Commissions of each day, if the Heart of the Mountain tier is below 10. Otherwise players earn an additional 1,600 ᠅ Mithril Powder , 3,200 ᠅ Gemstone Powder or 4,000 ᠅ Glacite Powder instead, depending on the area.
The Heart of the Mountain can be reset. This wipes all of the Heart of the Mountain upgrades and returns all spent ᠅ Mithril Powder , ᠅ Gemstone Powder , ᠅ Glacite Powder and Tokens of the Mountain . HotM tier and Core of the Mountain levels are kept; thus powder spent on upgrading Core of the Mountain is not reimbursed.

## Abilities
Heart of the Mountain Tiers 2, 6, and 10 offer 2 Pickaxe Abilities each, for a total of 6. They can all be unlocked on the tree at once, but only one can be selected at a time. They are activated with RIGHT CLICK , and have either an instant effect or a period of effect.
They have a cooldown, which starts immediately upon activation, not at the point of the ability's conclusion. The player must wait for the cooldown to expire before being able to use any other pickaxe ability. The cooldown is preserved across lobbies, and set to zero when entering a Glacite Mineshaft .
Pickaxe Abilities cannot be upgraded with powder, but they can be upgraded by unlocking Core of the Mountain and with Blue Cheese Goblin Omelettes .
- Mining Speed Boost
- Pickobulus
- Tunnel Vision
- Maniac Miner
- Gemstone Infusion
- Sheer Force
Mining Speed Boost is available upon reaching Heart of the Mountain Tier 2, however, it requires 3 Token of the Mountain to unlock, therefore it cannot be unlocked until Heart of the Mountain Tier 3.

#### Daily Powder
The first ore you mine each day grants +500 Powder, multiplied by your Heart of the Mountain level.

### Powder Cost Calculator

## Tips
- Use Pocket Iceberg to increase your Ⓟ Breaking Power by 1 .
- The recommended mining tools progressions are: Before entering ⏣ Dwarven Mines : Zombie , Promising , or Lapis Pickaxe . HotM 1: Rusty Titanium Pickaxe for Titanium ; Fractured Mithril Pickaxe for everything else HotM 2: Rusty Titanium Pickaxe for Titanium ; Mithril Pickaxe for everything else HotM 3: Titanium Pickaxe for Titanium ; Mithril Pickaxe or Mithril Drill SX-R226 for everything else (use a Pickaxe for things like Cobblestone , which are broken fast and in great quantities, but also not worth the fuel consumption) HotM 4: Polished Titanium Pickaxe for Titanium ; Ruby Drill TX-15 , Gemstone Drill LT-522 or Pickonimbus 2000 for Gemstones ; Jungle Pickaxe , Pickonimbus 2000 or Mithril Drill SX-R226 for Mithril and Pure Ores ; Jungle Pickaxe for everything else, especially Hard Stone . HotM 5: Polished Titanium Pickaxe for Titanium ; Topaz Drill KGR-12 for Gemstones ; Pickonimbus 2000 for Mithril and Pure Ores ; Jungle Pickaxe for everything else, especially Hard Stone . HotM 6: Titanium Drill DR-X655 can be used for everything, but Jasper Drill X is way more cost effective for Gemstones and Pickonimbus 2000 , Polished Titanium Pickaxe and Gemstone Gauntlet are good alternatives for other resources. HotM 7-10: Divan's Drill , but Titanium Drill DR-X655 and the ones mentioned above are more cost-effective.
- Before entering ⏣ Dwarven Mines : Zombie , Promising , or Lapis Pickaxe .
- HotM 1: Rusty Titanium Pickaxe for Titanium ; Fractured Mithril Pickaxe for everything else
- HotM 2: Rusty Titanium Pickaxe for Titanium ; Mithril Pickaxe for everything else
- HotM 3: Titanium Pickaxe for Titanium ; Mithril Pickaxe or Mithril Drill SX-R226 for everything else (use a Pickaxe for things like Cobblestone , which are broken fast and in great quantities, but also not worth the fuel consumption)
- HotM 4: Polished Titanium Pickaxe for Titanium ; Ruby Drill TX-15 , Gemstone Drill LT-522 or Pickonimbus 2000 for Gemstones ; Jungle Pickaxe , Pickonimbus 2000 or Mithril Drill SX-R226 for Mithril and Pure Ores ; Jungle Pickaxe for everything else, especially Hard Stone .
- HotM 5: Polished Titanium Pickaxe for Titanium ; Topaz Drill KGR-12 for Gemstones ; Pickonimbus 2000 for Mithril and Pure Ores ; Jungle Pickaxe for everything else, especially Hard Stone .
- HotM 6: Titanium Drill DR-X655 can be used for everything, but Jasper Drill X is way more cost effective for Gemstones and Pickonimbus 2000 , Polished Titanium Pickaxe and Gemstone Gauntlet are good alternatives for other resources.
- HotM 7-10: Divan's Drill , but Titanium Drill DR-X655 and the ones mentioned above are more cost-effective.
- The recommended mining armors progressions are: HotM 1 - 4: Glacite Armor or Yog Armor HotM 4 & 5: Sorrow Armor with at least Universal Slot unlocked is the best, but Yog Armor is more cost-effective and Heat Armor can be used for its Heat Immunity . HotM 6 - 10: Divan Armor with all slots unlocked is the best, but Sorrow Armor with at least Universal Slot unlocked is more cost effective and Heat Armor can be used for its Heat Immunity . Although Mineral and Glossy Mineral Armors should be used when mining Ores and Blocks . Equipment: HotM 2 & 3: Mithril Equipment HotM 4: Titanium Equipment HotM 5+: Titanium Equipment is the best for mining Titanium and Mithril in all areas and for everything while in ⏣ Dwarven Mines ( ⏣ Glacite Tunnels do not count as Dwarven Mines for this ability); Gemstone Equipment is better in every other instance, but is much, much more expensive. HotM 8+: Using 3/4 Titanium Equipment with Dwarven Handwarmers is an improvement over Full set of Titanium Eq. outside of ⏣ Dwarven Mines , and is the best available option when mining Mithril or Titanium outside of ⏣ Dwarven Mines . Using 3/4 Gemstone Equipment with Dwarven Handwarmers is better outside of ⏣ Crystal Hollows , and the best available option for mining resources that aren't Mithril or Titanium and are outside ⏣ Dwarven Mines . HotM 10: Using 2/4 Titanium Eq. , Dwarven Handwarmers and Pendant of Divan is the best setup for Mithril and Titanium . Using 2/4 Gemstone Eq. , Dwarven Handwarmers and Pendant of Divan is the best setup for everything else. Using 3/4 Gemstone Eq. with Pendant of Divan is the best setup in the game for Amethyst .
- HotM 1 - 4: Glacite Armor or Yog Armor
- HotM 4 & 5: Sorrow Armor with at least Universal Slot unlocked is the best, but Yog Armor is more cost-effective and Heat Armor can be used for its Heat Immunity .
- HotM 6 - 10: Divan Armor with all slots unlocked is the best, but Sorrow Armor with at least Universal Slot unlocked is more cost effective and Heat Armor can be used for its Heat Immunity .
- Although Mineral and Glossy Mineral Armors should be used when mining Ores and Blocks .
- Equipment: HotM 2 & 3: Mithril Equipment HotM 4: Titanium Equipment HotM 5+: Titanium Equipment is the best for mining Titanium and Mithril in all areas and for everything while in ⏣ Dwarven Mines ( ⏣ Glacite Tunnels do not count as Dwarven Mines for this ability); Gemstone Equipment is better in every other instance, but is much, much more expensive. HotM 8+: Using 3/4 Titanium Equipment with Dwarven Handwarmers is an improvement over Full set of Titanium Eq. outside of ⏣ Dwarven Mines , and is the best available option when mining Mithril or Titanium outside of ⏣ Dwarven Mines . Using 3/4 Gemstone Equipment with Dwarven Handwarmers is better outside of ⏣ Crystal Hollows , and the best available option for mining resources that aren't Mithril or Titanium and are outside ⏣ Dwarven Mines . HotM 10: Using 2/4 Titanium Eq. , Dwarven Handwarmers and Pendant of Divan is the best setup for Mithril and Titanium . Using 2/4 Gemstone Eq. , Dwarven Handwarmers and Pendant of Divan is the best setup for everything else. Using 3/4 Gemstone Eq. with Pendant of Divan is the best setup in the game for Amethyst .
- HotM 2 & 3: Mithril Equipment
- HotM 4: Titanium Equipment
- HotM 5+: Titanium Equipment is the best for mining Titanium and Mithril in all areas and for everything while in ⏣ Dwarven Mines ( ⏣ Glacite Tunnels do not count as Dwarven Mines for this ability); Gemstone Equipment is better in every other instance, but is much, much more expensive.
- HotM 8+: Using 3/4 Titanium Equipment with Dwarven Handwarmers is an improvement over Full set of Titanium Eq. outside of ⏣ Dwarven Mines , and is the best available option when mining Mithril or Titanium outside of ⏣ Dwarven Mines . Using 3/4 Gemstone Equipment with Dwarven Handwarmers is better outside of ⏣ Crystal Hollows , and the best available option for mining resources that aren't Mithril or Titanium and are outside ⏣ Dwarven Mines .
- HotM 10: Using 2/4 Titanium Eq. , Dwarven Handwarmers and Pendant of Divan is the best setup for Mithril and Titanium . Using 2/4 Gemstone Eq. , Dwarven Handwarmers and Pendant of Divan is the best setup for everything else. Using 3/4 Gemstone Eq. with Pendant of Divan is the best setup in the game for Amethyst .
- For almost any mining related action, there is a designated pet. Armadillo for mining Hard Stone . Bal for general mining (due to its 100 ☘ and 10% Pickaxe Cooldown reduction) but especially in ⏣ Magma Fields . Glacite Golem for mining inside the ⏣ Glacite Tunnels and moreso in ⏣ Glacite Mineshafts , and especially when grinding ᠅ Glacite Powder . Goblin for mining Ores , especially in ⏣ Mines of Divan . Mithril Golem for mining Mithril , grinding ᠅ Mithril Powder but also Combat related endeavours on Mining Islands. Mole for doing ⏣ Crystal Nucleus . Scatha for mining Gemstones , but also grinding ᠅ Gemstone Powder . Silverfish for levelling the Mining Skill . Snail for mining Blocks other than Hard Stone .
- Armadillo for mining Hard Stone .
- Bal for general mining (due to its 100 ☘ and 10% Pickaxe Cooldown reduction) but especially in ⏣ Magma Fields .
- Glacite Golem for mining inside the ⏣ Glacite Tunnels and moreso in ⏣ Glacite Mineshafts , and especially when grinding ᠅ Glacite Powder .
- Goblin for mining Ores , especially in ⏣ Mines of Divan .
- Mithril Golem for mining Mithril , grinding ᠅ Mithril Powder but also Combat related endeavours on Mining Islands.
- Mole for doing ⏣ Crystal Nucleus .
- Scatha for mining Gemstones , but also grinding ᠅ Gemstone Powder .
- Silverfish for levelling the Mining Skill .
- Snail for mining Blocks other than Hard Stone .

## Trivia
- Reaching Heart of the Mountain Tier 5 will reward the player with the "Core of the Mountain" Achievement .
- 2x Powder events also double Powder obtained from the Daily Powder perk, even though the message does not reflect this. This is now affected by the powder buff.
- This is now affected by the powder buff.
- If multiple pickaxe abilities are unlocked, one must be selected in order to be used. However players are able to switch an ability while another is under effect, leading to multiple being active at the same time.
- All Heart of the Mountain tier 7 perks cost the same amount of ᠅ Gemstone Powder .
- Despite being impossible to get every single perk in Heart of the Mountain, if one were to get all of them and max each one out (including Core of the Mountain), it would cost 12,808,220 ᠅ Mithril Powder , 32,550,666 ᠅ Gemstone Powder and 37,479,533 ᠅ Glacite Powder as well as 45 Tokens of the Mountain .
- The Heart of the Mountain is a reference to the Arkenstone from J.R.R. Tolkien's The Hobbit . The Arkenstone is the biggest and rarest gemstone in the Lonely Mountain, and valued most by the Dwarves.
- The Arkenstone is the biggest and rarest gemstone in the Lonely Mountain, and valued most by the Dwarves.
- Lonesome Miner 's perk also affects Legion , Superior Dragon Armor , Ender Dragon Pets and any other items that affects the buffed stats.
- Mole and Efficient Miner do not trigger within protected structures in the ⏣ Crystal Hollows . This includes structures that house Gemstone Crystals , and some generated structures.
- This includes structures that house Gemstone Crystals , and some generated structures.
- It is not possible to reset the Heart of the Mountain if the only unlocked perk is Mining Speed. Unlocking another perk will allow the player to reset it.
- The Sky Mall perk "Gain 15% powder while mining" does not buff powder gain from chests.
- Powder buff from Pets and Holding items are additive, but the one from King Talisman is multiplicative.
- The Maniac Miner perk is based on a team upgrade in Hypixel Bed Wars, which grants Haste 1 and 2.
- Some perks were renamed, removed, or moved to another HotM tier: The Quick Forge perk was moved from HotM 2 to HotM 3 next to the Pickobulus ability and Seasoned Mineman perk. The Daily Powder perk was moved from HotM 3 to HotM 5 next to the Seasoned Mineman and Great Explorer perks. The Crystallized perk was removed; this gains 200 ⸕ Mining Speed and having a 200% chance to deal more damage to a Star Sentry if you are near the Fallen Star . The Efficient Miner Perk was moved from HotM 4 to HotM 3 next to the Mining Fortune and Mole perks; this was also reworked due to the new stat in ▚ Mining Spread except Gemstones. The Orbiter perk was removed; this perk increases the chance to gain additional experience orbs upon mining ores. The Mining Madness perk was removed; this perk gains 50 ⸕ Mining Speed and 50 ☘ Mining Fortune without upgrading. The Precision Mining perk was moved from HotM 4 to HotM 2 due to this perk having Early-Game ⸕ Mining Speed . The Goblin Killer perk was removed; this perk gains ᠅ Mithril Powder depending on the Goblin type killed. The Star Powder perk was removed; this perk gains extra ᠅ Mithril Powder when mining near the Fallen Star. The Mole Perk was moved from HotM 6 to HotM 4; this perk was also reworked due to the new stat in ▚ Mining Spread when mining Hard Stone . The Fortunate Perk was reworked, renamed to Gem Lover, and moved from HotM 6 to HotM 4; this perk now grants ☘ Gemstone Fortune . The Vein Seeker ability was removed; this ability points in the direction of the nearest vein from a player is pointed and gains ▚ Mining Spread . The Mining Speed II and Mining Fortune II were renamed to Speedy Mineman and Fortunate Mineman respectively and nerfed.
- The Quick Forge perk was moved from HotM 2 to HotM 3 next to the Pickobulus ability and Seasoned Mineman perk.
- The Daily Powder perk was moved from HotM 3 to HotM 5 next to the Seasoned Mineman and Great Explorer perks.
- The Crystallized perk was removed; this gains 200 ⸕ Mining Speed and having a 200% chance to deal more damage to a Star Sentry if you are near the Fallen Star .
- The Efficient Miner Perk was moved from HotM 4 to HotM 3 next to the Mining Fortune and Mole perks; this was also reworked due to the new stat in ▚ Mining Spread except Gemstones.
- The Orbiter perk was removed; this perk increases the chance to gain additional experience orbs upon mining ores.
- The Mining Madness perk was removed; this perk gains 50 ⸕ Mining Speed and 50 ☘ Mining Fortune without upgrading.
- The Precision Mining perk was moved from HotM 4 to HotM 2 due to this perk having Early-Game ⸕ Mining Speed .
- The Goblin Killer perk was removed; this perk gains ᠅ Mithril Powder depending on the Goblin type killed.
- The Star Powder perk was removed; this perk gains extra ᠅ Mithril Powder when mining near the Fallen Star.
- The Mole Perk was moved from HotM 6 to HotM 4; this perk was also reworked due to the new stat in ▚ Mining Spread when mining Hard Stone .
- The Fortunate Perk was reworked, renamed to Gem Lover, and moved from HotM 6 to HotM 4; this perk now grants ☘ Gemstone Fortune .
- The Vein Seeker ability was removed; this ability points in the direction of the nearest vein from a player is pointed and gains ▚ Mining Spread .
- The Mining Speed II and Mining Fortune II were renamed to Speedy Mineman and Fortunate Mineman respectively and nerfed.

## History
  Alpha Hypixel Network
  June 30, 2021
  AHN 0.12 Round 1
  Added Heart of the Mountain Tiers 6 and 7.
  Added Lonesome Miner, Professional, Mole, Fortunate, Great Explorer, Vein Seeker, Maniac Miner, Mining Speed II, Powder Buff and Mining Fortune II perks.
  July 25, 2022
  Seasoned Mineman now gives ☯ Mining Wisdom .
  Sep 2, 2022
  AHN 0.15
  Heart of the Mountain now gives SkyBlock XP .
  July 3, 2025
  Removed cost of resetting the Heart of the Mountain tree.
  SkyBlock Prototype
  Jan 15, 2021
  0.11
  Added Heart of the Mountain.
  Jan 20, 2021
  Heart of the Mountain Tier 2 grants 1 additional Token of the Mountain.
  Fixed bug where pickaxe abilities would persist after a HotM reset.
  Fixed bug where HotM reset timer would count up instead of down.
  Goblin Killer perk now only increases the amount of powder received from Golden Goblin rather than all Goblins.
  Fixed pickaxe ability cooldowns resetting after switching servers.
  Precision Mining perk now gives +30% ⸕ Mining Speed instead of +300%.
  Heart of the Mountain menu can now be accessed via /hotm.
  Jan 27, 2021
  Mining Fortune perk now gives +5 ☘ Mining Fortune per level instead of +2.
  July 14, 2021
  0.12
  Added Heart of the Mountain Tiers 6 and 7.
  Added Lonesome Miner, Professional, Mole, Fortunate, Great Explorer, Vein Seeker, Maniac Miner, Mining Speed II, Powder Buff and Mining Fortune II perks.
  Reduced amount of HotM XP required to reach level 5 by 15,000 (from 75k to 60k).
  Daily Powder now gives Gemstone Powder upon mining Gemstone, in addition to Mithril Powder for Mithril.
  Doubled the amount of Powder gained from Daily Powder.
  +1500 ores for Front Loaded (from 1,000 to 2,500).
  July 16, 2021
  Peak of the Mountain is no longer a valid prerequisite for Mole.
  July 20, 2021
  Fixed issue where players who had between 60k and 75k HotM XP before the update were not granted their 2 Tokens.
  Efficient Miner is now a valid prerequisite for Mole.
  July 27, 2021
  Fixed Efficient Miner not mining as many blocks as it was supposed to.
  Efficient Miner now only mines blocks of the same type.
  Improved Mole's block breaking to no longer favor one direction.
  Fixed Powder Buff not working on loot chests.
  Aug 18, 2022
  0.14
  Seasoned Mineman now gives ☯ Mining Wisdom .
  Sep 28, 2022
  0.15
  Added Peak of the Mountain Tier 6 and 7.

## References

---

# Dwarven Mines

The Dwarven Mines is a location that is focused on Mining . It has several unique Dwarven Metals , including Mithril and Titanium : the Heart of the Mountain is also unlocked here.
Mining XII and completion of Rhys ' quest is required to access the Dwarven Mines .

## Overview
The primary focuses of the Dwarven Mines are to complete Commissions , which are tasks given by the King , to level up your Heart of the Mountain , and collect different varieties of Powder : that being ᠅ Mithril Powder , ᠅ Gemstone Powder , and ᠅ Glacite Powder .

## Tasks
When the player first enters ⏣ Dwarven Mines , they will be greeted with the following message:

## Navigation
Players will arrive in the ⏣ Dwarven Village , where Rhys can be found, as well as several commodities: Bubu sells pickaxes with various stats, Bulvar sells Tier 12 mining minions, Banker Broadjaw allows players to access their Bank , Lumina sells various light sources, Fragilis shows the Handy Block Guide, and Geo allows players to add Gemstones to their items.
The gate to the ⏣ Crystal Hollows can be found at Gwendolyn , who can be found at the outskirts of the Dwarven Village: after reaching Heart of the Mountain IV , the player can pay a coins fee to enter the Crystal Hollows for 6 hours.
Exiting the Dwarven Village will reveal a crossroads: the left path leads to the ⏣ Royal Palace via the ⏣ Palace Bridge , which overlooks the ⏣ Royal Mines ; the right path leads to the rest of the Dwarven Mines via the ⏣ Gates to the Mines , which overlooks ⏣ The Forge .
Beyond the ⏣ Great Ice Wall , the ⏣ Dwarven Base Camp can be found: it is inaccessible without Heart of the Mountain VII and completion of Dulin 's quest, which also grants permanent free entry to the ⏣ Crystal Hollows .

### Dwarven Mines Rail System
The Station Master can be found in the ⏣ Dwarven Village , with several Ticket Master s found around stations in the Dwarven Mines. After paying a small coins fee, depending on your proximity to your desired location, players can enter a minecart and travel to other areas around the Dwarven Mines .

## Events
Events will regularly happen around the Dwarven Mines every 20 minutes: they are either Active , Passive , or Minor .
  Name
  Type
  Description
  2x Powder
  Passive
  While is event is active, all ᠅ Mithril Powder , ᠅ Gemstone Powder , and ᠅ Glacite Powder obtained will be doubled .
  Gone with the Wind
  Passive
  While this event is active, mining in the direction of the wind grants increased ⸕ Mining Speed .
  Better Together
  Passive
  While this event is active, players gain increased ⸕ Mining Speed and ☘ Mining Fortune when they are in the same zone as another player, up to 5 players.
  Mithril Gourmand
  Active
  While this event is active, Don Expresso appears in the ⏣ Dwarven Tavern . Mining Mithril in a specified area has a chance to drop Tasty Mithril : 200 of this must be given to Don to complete the event, and giving at least 10 personally will grant extra rewards.
  Raffle
  Active
  While this event is active, a Raffle Box appears in a random location: Raffle Tickets will also spawn in the zone, and must be handed in to the Raffle Box before the event ends. The more tickets you deposit, the higher the chance of you winning the raffle and gaining increased rewards.
  Goblin Raid
  Active
  While this event is active, several hordes of Goblins will appear in a specified location and must be defeated within 5 minutes for participants to claim rewards.
  Fallen Star
  Minor
  A Fallen Star will randomly fall in a random location: Mithril , Titanium , and ᠅ Mithril Powder drops are increased, Starfall has a chance to be obtained, and Star Sentries will spawn.
  Powder Ghast
  Minor
  A Powder Ghast will appear in a random location and must be shot several times in order to be killed. Each successful shot grants ᠅ Mithril Powder .

## Trivia
- The map for the Dwarven Mines is internally called the Deeper Caverns .
- The Dwarven Mines were possibly initially called the Dwarven Caves. Trying to use the Royal Pigeon outside of the Dwarven Mines used to display the message, "You may not use this Item outside the Dwarven Caves!"
- There used to be a hole in the ceiling (located at 66, 222, -83) that would lead the player onto the roof of the mines, where there was text, written in blocks, that read: "WHY ARE YOU UP HERE?" "COS" "THE NERVE!"
- "WHY ARE YOU UP HERE?" "COS" "THE NERVE!"
- Before November 8, 2021 , players could use the command /warpforge to travel to The Forge , without having to consume a Travel Scroll. Since November 8, 2021, a Travel Scroll must be consumed in order for the command to function. Prior to the update, the command could also be used while combat tagged or as a spectator in Dungeons.

# Crystal Hollows

The Crystal Hollows is a location that is focused on Mining . The primary focuses of the Crystal Hollows are mining Gemstones and collecting Gemstone Crystals to complete the Crystal Nucleus .

## Tasks
When the player first enters ⏣ Crystal Hollows , they will be greeted with the following message:

## Overview
The Crystal Hollows consists of a large series of tunnels made of Hard Stone , with veins of Gemstones and randomly-generated structures scattered throughout the caves. The tunnels themselves remain the same across lobbies, but the locations of structures will always be different across different servers. At the center of the Crystal Hollows houses the ⏣ Crystal Nucleus , where Gemstone Crystals can be placed.
Talking to Gwendolyn allows you to purchase a pass to the Crystal Hollows for 6h for 10,000 coins : you gain permanent, unrestricted access to the Crystal Hollows after helping Dulin .

### Locations
There are 5 main locations in the Crystal Hollows , being the ⏣ Jungle , ⏣ Mithril Deposits , ⏣ Precursor Remnants , ⏣ Goblin Holdout , and ⏣ Magma Fields . These correspond to their respective Gemstone , that being Amethyst , Jade , Sapphire , Amber , and Topaz . Ruby can also be found in the Crystal Hollows and can be  found everywhere. Additionally, 3 ⏣ Fairy Grotto s spawn in random locations throughout the Crystal Hollows: Jasper can be mined there.
Each primary location has a sub-location, where its respective Gemstone Crystal can be obtained.
- The ⏣ Jungle contains the ⏣ Jungle Temple , where a Jungle Key must be given to access a series of parkour with the Amethyst Crystal at the end;
- The ⏣ Mithril Deposits contains the ⏣ Mines of Divan , where a Metal Detector must be used to find and return Scavenged Items , with the Jade Crystal being rewarded at the end;
- The ⏣ Precursor Remnants contains the ⏣ Lost Precursor City , where all 6 Automaton Parts or a Precursor Apparatus must be given to access the Sapphire Crystal ;
- The ⏣ Goblin Holdout contains the ⏣ Goblin Queen's Den , where any variant of Goblin Egg must be given to King Yolkar the Amber Crystal without being caught;
- The ⏣ Magma Fields contains ⏣ Khazad-dûm , where Bal must be defeated to claim the Topaz Crystal .
Gemstone Crystals can be placed in the ⏣ Crystal Nucleus to or used to forge Perfect Gemstones . You can see the status of Gemstone Crystals in the tablist: a Crystal can either be Not Found , Not Placed , or Placed . A Gemstone Crystal must be found but Not Placed to be used in the Forge to forge a its respective Perfect Gemstone.

### Mining
While inside the Crystal Hollows, broken ores and blocks are not replaced with bedrock. Instead, they will physically be broken be replaced with air, similar to vanilla Minecraft . Blocks can be broken everywhere except the ⏣ Crystal Nucleus and in specific structures: Torches , Ladders , and Hard Stone can also be placed.
Stone is replaced by Hard Stone inside the Crystal Hollows , which has a higher Ⓟ Breaking Power and a unique Collection. Gemstones , Mithril , and most Ores can spawn inside the Crystal Hollows. Ores that require a Furnace to be smelted into an ingot, such as Iron Ore and Gold Ore , do not require Smelting Touch or a Furnace to be converted to an ingot.
Yields from most vanilla ores are increased within the Crystal Hollows.
  Icon
  Ore
  Base Yield
  Coal Ore
  4x Coal
  Lapis Lazuli Ore
  9x Lapis Lazuli
  Redstone Ore
  22x Redstone
  Emerald Ore
  4x Emerald
  Diamond Ore
  4x Diamond

### Treasure and Loot Chests
Upon mining blocks, there is a small chance to spawn a treasure chest, containing various rewards. These chests can spawn anywhere except near the bedrock wall. The player must aim at the critical particles on the face of the chests 5 times in a row in order to open a chest. These treasure chests spawned from mining will only last for around 1 minute before disappearing.
Loot chests on the other hand can spawn in set locations within structures; these chests can be opened directly with a small time delay and contain about twice the gemstones and powder of what a treasure chest gives on average.
The loot within such a certain structure chest is always the same for all players who open it within that Crystal Hollows instance. However, the amount of Mithril and Gemstone Powder within each slot of the chest varies between players. Chests from mining do not share this property.
Treasure and Loot chests will only contain the loot found within the area. For example, Magma Fields chests might contain Yoggie , Topaz or Ruby .
Treasure and Loot chests have a 5% chance to be a rare loot chest, which can contain better drops. If the chest is not a rare loot chest, it will contain common loot.
The Crystal Serendipity attribute grants, at max level, a +20% chance to double rewards from a Treasure Chest. When this activates, the following message displays:
The possible loot is listed below, as well as the chance of the item being rolled as a drop from chests. 3-6 drops are rolled per chest.

### Possible Loot
- Jungle
- Goblin Holdout
- Mithril Deposits
- Precursor Remnants
- Magma Fields
- Fairy Grotto
- Crystal Hollows

## Structures
Each part of the Crystal Hollows has its own main special location, excluding Magma Fields , which will almost always generate in every lobby:
- The Jungle Temple generated in the Jungle
- The Mines of Divan generated in the Mithril Deposits
- The Goblin Queen's Den generated in the Goblin Holdout
- The Lost Precursor City generated in the Precursor Remnants
- 3 Fairy Grottos generated anywhere within the Crystal Hollows
Each of these structures house their respective Crystal . A special task must be completed to obtain the Crystal.
Khazad-dûm is the one location that can spawn in any part of the Crystal Hollows, making it harder to find.
There are also smaller structures which generate in random locations. Examples include:
- A structure which resembles the Deep Caverns , including the lift and the layered structure of the original Deep Caverns island
- A dragon skull from the Spider's Den
- A replica of the Dark Auction
- A miniature version of The Forge including a working forge NPC
- A copy of the pre- Hub overhaul Tavern
A full list of Structures can be found at Crystal Hollows/Special Locations .
Certain structures contain loot chests. Loot chests always generate in the same positions within the structures, similar to Dungeon Secrets . Loot Chests also generate the same items for every player, meaning if a player finds a chest with good loot such as a lot of Gemstone Powder or a Blue Goblin Egg, they can send the coordinates to chat to lead others to the chest.

## Trivia
- The Crystal Hollows are internally referred to as the Greater Mines in the SkyBlock API.
- The Crystal Hollows are the only place Dirt , Andesite , Diorite , and Granite (and other blocks) can be mined, however, only Dirt drops itself and all others drop Hard Stone instead.
- Ores within a few blocks of the Bedrock border may not get auto-smelted without Smelting Touch .
- Attempting to get into the Crystal Hollows using an Ender Pearl will result in the player being teleported out with the following message, even if they do have a valid Crystal Hollows Pass: You have been teleported out of the Crystal Hollows because you did not have a valid pass!
You have been teleported out of the Crystal Hollows because you did not have a valid pass!
- A player cannot claim rewards from the same loot chest on multiple profiles.

  Alpha Hypixel Network
  June 30, 2021
  AHN 0.12 Round 1
  Added Crystal Hollows .
  Unknown Date
  Changed size of the Crystal Hollows from 1024 x 256 x 1024 to 621 x 157 x 621.
  Unknown Date
  Fixed all Polished Diorite blocks within the Crystal Hollows counting as Titanium and regenerating.
  Aug 20, 2024
  Increased entry requirement from Heart of the Mountain Tier III -> IV.
  Removed ᠅ Mithril Powder from Crystal Hollows treasure and loot chests.
  SkyBlock Prototype
  July 14, 2021
  0.12
  Added Crystal Hollows .
  July 20, 2021
  Updated Hollows map to improve navigation slightly.
  Removed Ruby Skull Matching Puzzle room.
  Fixed not being able to fish up certain Crystal Hollows sea creatures.
  July 22, 2021
  Updated Jungle Temple to make the parkour easier.
  July 27, 2021
  Added a 5 minute spawn protection area around entrances.
  2 Fairy Grottos will spawn per lobby rather than 1.
  Improved warping to and from the Crystal Hollows.
  Improved pass checks.
  Reduced Powder amounts from loot chests.
  Fixed loot chest spawning in some rooms.
  Updated some rooms with context clues and spacing.
  Aug 24, 2021
  Added background soundtrack.
  Unknown Date
  Extended the duration of the Crystal Hollows pass to 5 hours.
  Nov 8, 2021
  Newer Crystal Hollows servers will now be prioritised when entering the Crystal Hollows.
  The Crystal Hollows now remains open for 5 hours, or 15 in-game days (from 2 hours, or 6 in-game days).
  3 Fairy Grottos now spawn per lobby rather than 2.
  When the player enters the Crystal Hollows via a warp (not the Minecart track) it will now put them at a random entrance.
  Apr 9, 2022
  Disabled Loot Chests.
  Apr 13, 2022
  Re-enabled Loot Chests.
  Loot Chests now immediately give the loot after opening rather than opening a Chest GUI.
  Feb 14, 2023
  0.18
  Extended the duration of the Crystal Hollows pass to 6 hours.
  June 26, 2023
  Added a cooldown to some warning messages in Crystal Hollows .
  Fixed always respawning at the same entrance in Crystal Hollows when dying.
  Sep 17, 2024
  0.20.6
  Increased entry requirement from Heart of the Mountain Tier III -> IV.
  Removed ᠅ Mithril Powder from Crystal Hollows treasure and loot chests.

# Gemstone Gauntlet

The Gemstone Gauntlet is a LEGENDARY Gauntlet.

## Stats
  Gauntlet V E D
  Gemstone Gauntlet ❁ Damage : +300 Ⓟ Breaking Power : +8 ⸕ Mining Speed : +800 ❁ Strength : +50
- ❁ Damage : +300
- Ⓟ Breaking Power : +8
- ⸕ Mining Speed : +800
- ❁ Strength : +50
  Effects
  Ability: Reduced To Atoms Kill mobs on Mining Islands to charge the Gauntlet Meter . Mobs killed drop the same Gemstone type as your filled Gemstone Slots. (2s cooldown) Ability: Kinetic Killing a mob on a Mining Island reduces all of your Forge Timers by 0s . (+0.5s per Perfect Gemstone)

## Crafting
  Requirements
  Ingredients
  Crafting recipe
  Gemstone XI
  8x Flawless Ruby Gemstone 16x Enchanted Gold Block
- 8x Flawless Ruby Gemstone
- 16x Enchanted Gold Block
  16

## Tips
- The Gemstone Gauntlet can be used to easily kill mobs in ⏣ Glacite Mineshafts , dealing much more damage than a drill, meaning a damage power stone may not be necessary.
- It is recommended to have a high amount of ✧ Pristine to increase the drops from the Reduced to Atoms ability.
- To reach 9 Ⓟ Breaking Power , to be able to mine all the mining resources, a Pocket Iceberg can be applied to the Gemstone Gauntlet , while also granting it some ☘ Mining Fortune and ☯ Mining Wisdom .

## Trivia
- This item is a reference to the Infinity Gauntlet from Marvel's Avengers franchise.
- Upon placing all 5 gemstones into the item for the first time, the player will be awarded the "I call that... Mercy" Achievement . The name of the achievement is a quote by Thanos .
- The name of the achievement is a quote by Thanos .
- Players without Heart of the Mountain VI can still apply Gemstones to the Gemstone Gauntlet .
- For mere 2 days after 0.20.6 update, it had a third ability called the Gemstone Snap , it required the player to kill 150 mobs in mining islands in exchange for an ability that grants +50 ☘ Mining Fortune for 60 minutes . This was removed, cited as to improve server performance due to the large item lore, and the ability found to be annoying by players.
- Like Pickaxes and Drills , it can damage ❆ Glacial mobs. Due to functioning as a both Pickaxe and a Sword , its Damage is amplified, especially with enchantments.
- Due to functioning as a both Pickaxe and a Sword , its Damage is amplified, especially with enchantments.
- Despite having a slot at the top, which is revealed to be white when fully maxed, the Gemstone Gauntlet cannot have an Opal Gemstone equipped.
- Some of its gemstone slots are not helpful and effectively only serve for the visual effect.
- Despite being so cheap, it is the 3rd best generalist mining tool after the Divan's Drill and Titanium Drill DR-X655 . A Titanium Drill DR-X355 with a Ruby-Polished Drill Engine or a Titanium Drill DR-X455 without an engine outclasses it for non-gemstone mining, while the Jasper Drill X outclasses it for gemstone mining.
- A Titanium Drill DR-X355 with a Ruby-Polished Drill Engine or a Titanium Drill DR-X455 without an engine outclasses it for non-gemstone mining, while the Jasper Drill X outclasses it for gemstone mining.
- The Gemstone Gauntlet has as many slots as the Mastiff Armor , Divan's Drill and Armor of Divan . The Relic of Power (12) and the Shimmersparkle Chestplate (20) can hold more.
- For a short while, during the testing of Some Mining Changes on the Alpha Hypixel Network , this item was classified as "Sword and Pickaxe" rather than the Gauntlet it was always classified on the main network.
- The Gemstone Gauntlet is one of the items that can have two stacking enchantments ( Champion and Compact ). The other ones are Melon Dicer and Pumpkin Dicer ( Cultivating and Absorb ).

## Gallery
When a slot is filled by a Perfect Gemstone, the texture will change to show it applied. When all 5 Perfect Gemstones are added to the Gauntlet, it will change appearance from dark gray to gold.
In total, there are 32 different appearances for this item. These are all the Gemstone Gauntlets with different slots filled by perfect gemstones.
